### ResolverActivationReportValidationMatrix

`ResolverActivationReportValidationMatrix` validates promotion eligibility for active identity resolver catalogs. Rows with `TODO:` fixture or expected checksum values are blockers and must not be marked passing. A scenario row may pass only when the scenario fixture checksum, expected decision checksum, expected explanation checksum, expected review/handoff/error checksum, selected resolver catalog refs, package-set refs when package-supplied, and `030.VersionManifest` refs are concrete and non-`TODO:`.

| scenario_id | fixture_checksum | expected_decision_checksum | expected_explanation_checksum | expected_review_or_handoff_refs | expected_error_or_no_op_checksum | package_set_requirement | version_manifest_requirement | result | promotion_eligibility |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `activation-070-creation` | `TODO: creation fixture checksum required` | `TODO: creation decision checksum required` | `TODO: creation explanation checksum required` | none | `TODO: weak-only creation rejection checksum required` | required when package-supplied | resolver row, evidence class row, scope row, candidate profile, decision row, confidence band, explanation policy, output refs | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-attachment` | `TODO: attachment fixture checksum required` | `TODO: attachment decision checksum required` | `TODO: attachment explanation checksum required` | none | `TODO: two-canonical attachment rejection checksum required` | required when package-supplied | full resolver catalog refs and selected output refs | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-durable-merge` | `TODO: durable merge fixture checksum required` | `TODO: durable merge decision checksum required` | `TODO: durable merge explanation checksum required` | none | `TODO: blocker-precedence rejection checksum required` | required when package-supplied | full resolver catalog refs and selected output refs | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-weak-evidence-rejection` | `TODO: weak evidence fixture checksum required` | `TODO: weak rejection decision checksum required` | `TODO: weak rejection explanation checksum required` | no review unless policy permits | `TODO: weak no-mutation checksum required` | required when package-supplied | weak evidence class rows, decision rows, confidence bands, selector policy, output refs | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-blocker-precedence` | `TODO: blocker precedence fixture checksum required` | `TODO: blocker decision checksum required` | `TODO: blocker explanation checksum required` | blocker fixture refs | `TODO: blocker diagnostic checksum required` | required when package-supplied | hard blocker rows, generation boundary rows, decision rows, explanation refs | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-overflow` | `TODO: overflow fixture checksum required` | `TODO: overflow decision checksum required` | `TODO: overflow explanation checksum required` | overflow error refs | `TODO: overflow error checksum required` | required when package-supplied | candidate profile refs and overflow diagnostics | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-review-totality` | `TODO: review totality fixture checksum required` | `TODO: terminal review decision checksum required` | `TODO: terminal review explanation checksum required` | review case refs | `TODO: illegal-transition no-op checksum required` | required when package-supplied | review policy refs, state-machine checksum, transition evidence refs | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-split-handoff` | `TODO: split handoff fixture checksum required` | `TODO: split decision checksum required` | `TODO: split explanation checksum required` | graph correction handoff refs | `TODO: no-direct-graph-mutation checksum required` | required when package-supplied | split policy, affected fact, partition, explanation, handoff, and manifest refs | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-selector-safety` | `TODO: selector safety fixture checksum required` | `TODO: selector decision checksum required` | `TODO: selector explanation checksum required` | unresolved target refs | `TODO: selector unsafe or no-op checksum required` | required when package-supplied | target selector policy row refs, unresolved target refs, graph endpoint blocker refs when visible | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-explanation-checksum-replay` | `TODO: explanation replay fixture checksum required` | `TODO: replay decision checksum required` | `TODO: replay explanation checksum required` | explanation refs | `TODO: volatile-field exclusion checksum required` | required when package-supplied | explanation policy, all included field refs, manifest refs | blocked | not_eligible |
| `activation-070-shadow-canary-determinism` | `TODO: shadow/canary fixture checksum required` | `TODO: shadow/canary decision checksum required` | `TODO: shadow/canary explanation checksum required` | resolver shadow run refs | `TODO: shadow/canary mismatch checksum required` | required when package-supplied | production, shadow, and canary resolver refs and output checksums | blocked | not_eligible |

A report is promotion-eligible only when every required scenario row is `pass`, every checksum is non-`TODO:`, every selected resolver artifact ref is active and validation-backed, every required review or handoff ref is manifest-included, and every package-supplied row or validation artifact is included in the active `100.ProductionPackageSetManifest`. Candidate activation failure must preserve the current active package set.

### Acceptance Criteria

| ID | Criterion |
| --- | --- |

### Structured input validation acceptance criteria

| ID | Criterion |
| --- | --- |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-AC-001` | `AcceptanceReport` cannot pass while any structured-input validation row is `blocked`, `not_run`, `fail`, stale, checksum-mismatched, or `TODO`. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-AC-002` | Exact same repository snapshot inputs produce byte-identical validation output. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-AC-003` | Merge to repository alone produces no production mutation. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-AC-004` | Materialized package activation requires allowed repository form, materialization refs, package release refs, package-set refs, and `VersionManifest` refs. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-TEMPLATE-AC-001` | Template conformance positive and negative rows prove layout validation and template non-authority. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-TOOL-AC-001` | SDK/CLI rows prove deterministic invocation, version mismatch rejection, generated output drift rejection, and tool success non-authority. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-CI-AC-001` | Producer CI rows prove exact-snapshot binding, stale-CI rejection, CI success non-authority, and CI private leak rejection. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-PUBLICATION-AC-001` | Publication rows prove import success, digest mismatch rejection, package type mismatch rejection, and compatibility claim mismatch rejection. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-SYNC-AC-001` | Sync rows prove candidate discovery, stale sync rejection, sync-only activation failure, and rollback mutable-ref rejection. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-MULTIREPO-AC-001` | Multi-repository rows prove coherent group success, group mismatch rejection, and partial group activation rejection. |
| `120-STRUCTURED-INPUT-WORKFLOW-CLOSURE-AC-001` | `AcceptanceReport.result = pass` remains impossible while any structured-input workflow row is `blocked`, `not_run`, `fail`, stale, checksum-mismatched, package-set-mismatched, manifest-incomplete, or `TODO`-bearing. |

## Definition of Done

| ID | Criterion |
| --- | --- |
| `120-SCOPE-SELECTOR-CLOSURE-AC-001` | Every active scoped owner family provides exact-match, subset-allowed, subset-disallowed, duplicate-dimension, duplicate-value, private-leak, missing-row, ambiguous-row, owner-error-mapping, redaction, and manifest-inclusion fixtures. |
| `120-SCOPE-SELECTOR-CLOSURE-AC-002` | `AcceptanceReport.result = pass` is forbidden when any active scoped owner family lacks required `ScopeSelectorValidationMatrix` fixture coverage. |
| `120-AC-001` | Every domain NLSpec has binary acceptance criteria and validation matrix rows for success, rejection, no-op, and edge behavior. |
| `120-AC-002` | Every required negative authority-boundary case is executable and produces the expected owner-specific error code. |
| `120-AC-003` | Golden corpus replay produces byte-identical expected outputs or deterministic failure records. |
| `120-AC-004` | Validation artifacts are redacted, checksummed, and replayable. |
| `120-AC-005` | The aggregate acceptance report is sufficient to decide whether the NLSpec set can be promoted to `authoritative`. |
| `120-AC-006` | `RunValidationMatrix` emits blocked or fail for any unresolved active feed category, unresolved profile branch, missing fixture checksum, or missing expected output checksum. |
| `120-AC-007` | Authoritative promotion is forbidden while any non-deferred identity closure row is `fail`, `blocked`, `not_run`, missing checksum, or has a `TODO` expected output. |
| `120-AC-008` | `AcceptanceReport.result = pass` requires every activation-catalog closure validation row to pass, no row to contain `TODO`, every owner row to be present, every fixture checksum to be concrete, and every expected output or expected error checksum to match observed bytes. |

### Observable API Error Selection Validation Matrix

This matrix validates `110.ErrorRecordSchema`, `110.GenerateErrorCodeRegistry`, and `110.SelectObservableError`. A row may pass only when fixture checksum, input checksum, generated registry checksum, owner fragment refs, expected emitted `ErrorRecord` array checksum, expected suppressed-candidate summary checksum, mutation-prohibition proof, and `030.VersionManifest` refs are concrete and non-`TODO`.

| validation_row_id | owner_spec | scenario | fixture_checksum | expected error or output | expected_output_checksum | mutation_prohibition | version_manifest_requirement | acceptance_criterion | blocking_status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `val-110-error-record-schema-legacy-code-rejected` | `110` | Caller-visible error row uses legacy top-level `code` or owner-specific top-level fields. | `TODO: product governance must supply fixture checksum` | `ERROR_REGISTRY_OWNER_FRAGMENT_INCOMPLETE` | `TODO: product governance must supply expected error checksum` | no response visibility with invalid error shape | generated registry checksum and registry validation refs included | `110-ERROR-RECORD-SCHEMA-AC-002` | blocked |
| `val-110-error-record-message-default` | `110` | Generated registry row omits `message_template`. | `TODO: product governance must supply fixture checksum` | emitted `ErrorRecord.message` equals `error_code` exactly | `TODO: product governance must supply expected output checksum` | no raw owner context in message | generated registry checksum included | `110-ERROR-RECORD-SCHEMA-AC-002` | blocked |
| `val-110-error-selection-owner-specific-before-generic` | `110`, owner specs | Owner-specific failure and shared generic fallback are both candidate-visible. | `TODO: product governance must supply fixture checksum` | owner-specific `ErrorRecord` is primary; shared generic is suppressed or supplemental only when permitted | `TODO: product governance must supply expected output checksum` | no generic substitute | registry checksum plus owner fragment refs included | `110-OBSERVABLE-ERROR-SELECTION-AC-001` | blocked |
| `val-110-error-selection-authorization-suppresses-owner-detail` | `110` | Authorization denial coincides with source, identity, graph, package, or evidence owner failure. | `TODO: product governance must supply fixture checksum` | caller-visible primary is `AUTHORIZATION_ERROR` or exact raw-payload permission code; existence-revealing owner detail is audit-only | `TODO: product governance must supply expected output checksum` | no existence leak | authorization decision, redaction context, registry checksum, and audit refs included | `110-OBSERVABLE-ERROR-SELECTION-AC-001` | blocked |
| `val-110-error-selection-page-token-before-owner-execution` | `110` | Invalid, expired, or mismatched page token is supplied with an otherwise valid owner request. | `TODO: product governance must supply fixture checksum` | exact page-token error selected and owner execution does not run | `TODO: product governance must supply expected error checksum` | no owner mutation or existence leak | page-token context refs and registry checksum included | `110-OBSERVABLE-ERROR-SELECTION-AC-001` | blocked |
| `val-110-error-selection-registry-checksum-omitted` | `110`, `030` | Visible diagnostic output omits `VersionManifest.generated_error_registry_checksum`. | `TODO: product governance must supply fixture checksum` | `VERSION_MANIFEST_INCOMPLETE` or generated registry failure before visibility | `TODO: product governance must supply expected error checksum` | no visible diagnostic without manifest proof | missing checksum detected before response visibility | `110-ERROR-REGISTRY-TOTAL-AC-001` | blocked |
| `val-110-error-selection-error-array-cap` | `110` | More than 128 caller-visible error candidates remain after redaction. | `TODO: product governance must supply fixture checksum` | first 128 sorted `ErrorRecord` rows emitted, `partial_result = true`, omitted-count summary audit-only | `TODO: product governance must supply expected output checksum` | no unsorted or unbounded error output | registry checksum, audit refs, and response checksum included | `110-OBSERVABLE-ERROR-SELECTION-AC-001` | blocked |

## Open Questions

Open questions marked `TODO:` block authoritative status for the affected contract. A downstream implementation must not resolve a `TODO:` by inference.

| ID | Question | Blocking scope | Required owner decision | Default until resolved |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `120-TODO-COVERAGE-DOMAIN-FIXTURE-CHECKSUMS` | TODO: Provide concrete fixture checksums, input checksums, expected output checksums, expected error checksums, mutation-prohibition proofs, and manifest refs for every `120-COVERAGE-DOMAIN-*` fixture row. | Coverage-domain token closure, feed-category token mapping, package-supplied coverage row catalogs, generated error registry parity, API rejection, and manifest inclusion. | Product validation owners for `020`, `030`, `060`, `100`, `110`, and `120`. | Acceptance aggregation returns `blocked` for `120-COVERAGE-DOMAIN-*`; promotion remains forbidden. |
| `120-TODO-GRAPH-POSTGRES-AGE-FIXTURE-CHECKSUMS` | TODO: Provide concrete fixture checksums, input checksums, expected output checksums, expected error checksums, mutation-prohibition proofs, provider support refs, package-set refs, restore/upgrade refs, benchmark thresholds, and manifest refs for every `120-GRAPH-POSTGRES-*`, `120-GRAPH-AGE-*`, and graph benchmark row. | PostgreSQL relational default, optional AGE validation profile, graph backend health, package gates, API error parity, telemetry redaction, restore/upgrade validation, and benchmark adequacy. | Product validation owners for `090`, `100`, `110`, `120`, `130`, and `140`. | Acceptance aggregation returns `blocked` for PostgreSQL/AGE graph backend rows until concrete refs and thresholds are supplied. |
| `120-TODO-API-ERROR-SELECTION-FIXTURE-CHECKSUMS` | TODO: Provide concrete fixtures, input checksums, generated registry checksums, expected emitted `ErrorRecord` arrays, expected suppressed-candidate summaries, expected response checksums, and mutation-prohibition proofs for every `val-110-error-*` row. | Error record schema, generated error registry parity, endpoint error precedence, authorization no-existence-leak behavior, page-token pre-execution rejection, and 128-error cap behavior. | Product validation owners for `030`, `110`, and `120`, plus affected owner specs that emit candidate failures. | Acceptance aggregation returns `blocked` for `val-110-error-*`; promotion remains forbidden when visible diagnostics are in implementation scope. |
